# Do not change tags in here without changing every other reference to them.
# If adding new groups or cultures, make sure they are unique.

# changes Jan 2018 :
# - New human culture group: culture_group_northmen
# - New elven culture group: culture_group_aumanyar, as in the silmarilien mod (for wood elves)
# - Removed culture_doriathrim, culture_eglath, and culture_mithrim, since these first age Sindar subgroups are
# Silmarilien specififc and don't appear in the character histories.
# - Commented out culture_wargs, until such time as someone decides to implement them fully
# - Added culture_sirannar in culture_group_aumanyar (as in the Silmarilien mod)
# - Deleted culture_boradin, the history files have been altered to culture_baradhrim. The Silmarilien mod
# makes a distinction between good (culture_boradin), bad (culture_ulbandim), and ancestral (culture_baradhrim),
# but for the 2nd age Eraidor, and a few historical characters, this distinction is not needed.
# - Replaced the Hungarian names for male culture_baradhrim with names more like those in the character histories
# - Added culture_edain_eraidor to culture_group_edain to represent the Second age Edain of Eraidor before the
# Numenoreans.
# - Added culture_edain_wilderland to culture_group_edain to for those relatives of 'The House of Hador' who
# lived east of the Misty Mountains and became close allies with the Longbeards early 2nd age ('Of Dwarves and Men').
# - Added culture_arvandor to culture_group_edain. They are from MERP, and fill a gap between the areas settled
# by culture_edain_wilderland and the Misty Mountains.
# - Removed culture_anach since it does not seem to have any place outside first age Beleriand.
# - Added culture_helmivalmistajat to culture_group_forodwaith, from the Silmarilien mod.
# - Added culture_kul_uruk 'Ice-Orcs' from the Silmarilien Mod (according to MERP, they lasted)

	# As described in the essay 'Of Dwarves and Men', these relatives of the house of Hador lived in 'Wilderland'
	# (east of the Northern Misty Mountains) from the First Age until the mid Second Age. They became close friends
	# of the Longbeards (to the extent that the Dwarves adopted thier language and names, which they kept long after
	# the original Human culture was destroyed).
	culture_edain_wilderland = {
		graphical_cultures = { hillmengfx }
		
		color = { 0.76 0.12 0.93 }
		
		male_names = {

	# From MERP, these were Edain-relatives who lived in what later became Rhudaur. They fit between the
	# dwarf-friends of the east, the Edain who later met with the Númeóreans to the west.
	# The Names need to be revised, of course...
